[DeviceFarm] APPIUM_LOG="$DEVICEFARM_LOG_DIR/appium.log"
nohup appium \
  --port=4723 \
  --relaxed-security \
  --allow-insecure=chromedriver_autodownload \
  --log-timestamp \
  --local-timezone \
  --log-level=debug > $APPIUM_LOG 2>&1 &
for i in {1..30}; do
  if curl --silent --connect-timeout 1 "http://127.0.0.1:4723/status" | grep -q "ready"; then
    echo "Appium started successfully"
    break
  fi
  echo "Waiting for Appium to start... ($i/30)"
  sleep 1
done
if ! curl --silent --fail "http://127.0.0.1:4723/status"; then
  echo "Appium failed to start. Logs:"
  cat $APPIUM_LOG
  exit 1
fi
